    <script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Get the current URL without any query parameters
    const path = window.location.pathname;
    // Check for the token parameter
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
    const token = urlParams.get('token');

    if (token !== null) { // Only proceed if token is present
        let funnelName = null;
        let eventName = null;

        // Determine funnel name based on URL path
        if (path.includes('/contact-us/confirmation')) {
            funnelName = 'contact-us';
            eventName = 'contact-centers';
        } else if (path.includes('/book-a-tour/confirmation')) {
            funnelName = 'book-a-tour';
            eventName = 'centers-registration-confirmation';
        }

        // If a valid funnel name was determined, push to dataLayer
        if (funnelName) {
            window.dataLayer = window.dataLayer || [];
            window.dataLayer.push({
                'event': eventName,
                'funnel_name': funnelName,
                'funnel_step': 2,
            });

            console.log('datalayer pushed');
        }
    }
});

    </script>

<script>
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Get the current URL without any query parameters
    const baseURL = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname;

    // Only proceed if we're on the right page and the 'populate' parameter exists
    if (baseURL === 'https://littlefootprints.edu.sg/blog') {
        // Get the populate parameter value
        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);
        const populateValue = urlParams.get('populate');

        if (populateValue) { // Only proceed if populate has a value
            let count = 0;

            const newsroomList = document.querySelector('.newsroom__list');
            const newsroomEmpty = document.querySelector('.newsroom__empty');

            if (newsroomList) { 
                // If results are present, count the number of newsroom__row classes
                count = document.querySelectorAll('.newsroom__row').length;
            } else if (newsroomEmpty) { 
                // If no results, set count to 0
                count = 0;
            }

            const inputValue = document.querySelector('[data-drupal-selector="edit-populate"]').value;
            
            dataLayer.push({
                'event': 'content-filter',
                'search_results': count,
                'search_terms': inputValue,
            });

            console.log('datalayer pushed with input value: '+inputValue+' and count: '+count);
        }
    }
});


document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Get the current URL without any query parameters
    const baseURL = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname;

    // Check if we're on the desired page
    if (baseURL === 'https://littlefootprints.edu.sg/webform/inscription_newsletter/confirmation') {

        dataLayer.push({
            'event': 'newsletter-subscription',
            'eventParameter1':'footer',
            'eventParameter2': 'confirmation page',
        });

            console.log('newsletter datalayer pushed');
    }
});


// Function to handle the click event
function handleNewsletterButtonClick() {

    // Push the event to the data layer
    dataLayer.push({
        'event': 'newsletter-subscription',
        'eventParameter1':'footer',
    });
}

// Wait for the DOM to be fully loaded
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Select the button with the class 'button-newsletter'
    const newsletterButton = document.querySelector('.button-newsletter');

    // Make sure the button exists
    if (newsletterButton) {
        // Add a click event listener to the button
        newsletterButton.addEventListener('click', handleNewsletterButtonClick);
    } else {
        console.error('Newsletter button not found.');
    }
});


document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
    // Get the current URL parts
    const baseURL = window.location.origin + window.location.pathname;
    const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);

    // Check if we're on a blog article page
    if (baseURL.startsWith('https://littlefootprints.edu.sg/blog/') && baseURL !== 'https://littlefootprints.edu.sg/blog' && !urlParams.has('populate')) {
        
        const tagsListElement = document.querySelector('.article__tags-item-list');
        
        if (tagsListElement) {
            const tagsElements = document.querySelectorAll('.article__tags-item');
            let concatenatedTags = Array.from(tagsElements).map(tag => tag.textContent.trim()).join(',');
              window.dataLayer.push({
                    'event': 'pageview',
                    'article_tags': concatenatedTags,
                });
            console.log(concatenatedTags); // Outputs: "CHILDCARE & PRESCHOOL,EDUCATION,PARENTING"
        }
    }
